```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline

    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    sr = sc = gr = gc = -1
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            c = grid[i][j]
            if c == 'S':
                sr, sc = i, j
            elif c == 'G':
                gr, gc = i, j
            elif c == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    # Special nodes: start + candies + goal
    k = len(candies)
    # Node indices:
    # 0: start
    # 1..k: candies
    # k+1: goal
    N = k + 2
    pos = [(sr, sc)] + candies + [(gr, gc)]

    INF = 10**18

    def bfs_from(sr0, sc0):
        dist = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
        q = deque()
        dist[sr0][sc0] = 0
        q.append((sr0, sc0))
        while q:
            r, c = q.popleft()
            nd = dist[r][c] + 1
            for dr, dc in ((1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)):
                nr, nc = r + dr, c + dc
                if 0 <= nr < H and 0 <= nc < W and dist[nr][nc] == -1:
                    if grid[nr][nc] != '#':
                        dist[nr][nc] = nd
                        q.append((nr, nc))
        return dist

    # Precompute pairwise shortest paths among special nodes
    d = [[INF] * N for _ in range(N)]
    # BFS from each special node
    bfs_dists = []
    for (r0, c0) in pos:
        bfs_dists.append(bfs_from(r0, c0))

    for i in range(N):
        for j in range(N):
            if i == j:
                d[i][j] = 0
            else:
                rr, cc = pos[j]
                val = bfs_dists[i][rr][cc]
                if val != -1:
                    d[i][j] = val

    # If goal unreachable at all from start within T, still might be possible via candies?
    # So just run DP; however, we can early exit only if start->goal is INF.
    # DP will cover other routes; no unsafe pruning beyond unreachable pairs.

    # DP over candy subsets:
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal travel cost starting from start, visiting candies in mask,
    # ending at candy 'last' (last is an index 0..k-1 corresponding to candy node 1+last).
    # We will finally add distance(last->goal) to check <= T.
    if k == 0:
        ans = d[0][N-1]
        if ans <= T:
            print(0)
        else:
            print(-1)
        return

    size = 1 << k
    dp = [ [INF]*k for _ in range(size) ]

    # Initialize: start -> each candy
    for last in range(k):
        dist = d[0][1 + last]
        if dist < INF:
            dp[1 << last][last] = dist

    # Transitions
    for mask in range(size):
        for last in range(k):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # try adding a new candy
            rem = (~mask) & (size - 1)
            while rem:
                lb = rem & -rem
                nxt = (lb.bit_length() - 1)
                ndist = d[1 + last][1 + nxt]
                if ndist < INF:
                    nmask = mask | lb
                    nc = cur + ndist
                    if nc < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                        dp[nmask][nxt] = nc
                rem -= lb

    # Evaluate answer: among all masks and last, with dp[mask][last] + dist(last->goal) <= T
    # Also allow visiting zero candies: start->goal.
    best = -1

    # Zero candy case
    if d[0][N-1] <= T:
        best = 0

    for mask in range(size):
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= best:
            continue
        for last in range(k):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            to_goal = d[1 + last][N-1]
            if to_goal == INF:
                continue
            if cur + to_goal <= T:
                best = max(best, cnt)

    print(best)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()

<summary>Augmented generation 4</summary>

```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

INF = 10**18

def bfs_from(grid, H, W, sr, sc):
    dist = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque([(sr, sc)])
    dist[sr][sc] = 0
    dirs = [(1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)]
    while q:
        r, c = q.popleft()
        d = dist[r][c] + 1
        for dr, dc in dirs:
            nr, nc = r + dr, c + dc
            if 0 <= nr < H and 0 <= nc < W and dist[nr][nc] == -1 and grid[nr][nc] != '#':
                dist[nr][nc] = d
                q.append((nr, nc))
    return dist

def solve():
    input = sys.stdin.readline
    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    specials = []  # 0: S, 1: G, others: candies
    sr = sc = gr = gc = None
    candy_positions = []

    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            ch = grid[i][j]
            if ch == 'S':
                sr, sc = i, j
            elif ch == 'G':
                gr, gc = i, j
            elif ch == 'o':
                candy_positions.append((i, j))

    specials.append((sr, sc))
    specials.append((gr, gc))
    specials.extend(candy_positions)
    N = len(specials)  # <= 20

    # Compute pairwise shortest-path distances among special nodes
    dmat = [[INF] * N for _ in range(N)]
    for i in range(N):
        sr, sc = specials[i]
        dist = bfs_from(grid, H, W, sr, sc)
        for j in range(N):
            tr, tc = specials[j]
            dd = dist[tr][tc]
            if dd != -1:
                dmat[i][j] = dd

    # Early check: if even S->G is unreachable or too long, still we must answer -1
    if dmat[0][1] > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Candies are indices 2..N-1 (count = K)
    K = N - 2
    if K == 0:
        # No candies, just need S->G within T
        print(0)
        return

    # Held-Karp bitmask DP: dp[mask][last] = minimal distance from S to node 'last'
    # after visiting candies in 'mask' (last is one of candies), without the final leg to G.
    size = 1 << K
    dp = [[INF] * K for _ in range(size)]

    # Initialize from S to each candy
    for c in range(K):
        dist_sc = dmat[0][2 + c]
        if dist_sc < INF:
            dp[1 << c][c] = dist_sc

    # Transitions
    for mask in range(size):
        for last in range(K):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur >= INF:
                continue
            # Try to go to next candy
            for nxt in range(K):
                if mask >> nxt & 1:
                    continue
                nd = dmat[2 + last][2 + nxt]
                if nd >= INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | (1 << nxt)
                nv = cur + nd
                if nv < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = nv

    # Evaluate: for each (mask, last), add shortest distance last->G
    ans = 0
    for mask in range(size):
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= ans:
            continue
        for last in range(K):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur >= INF:
                continue
            to_goal = dmat[2 + last][1]
            if to_goal >= INF:
                continue
            if cur + to_goal <= T:
                ans = cnt
                break

    # Also consider taking zero candies: already checked S->G <= T, so ans >= 0
    print(ans)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()

<summary>Augmented generation 5</summary>

```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

INF = 10**18

def bfs_dist(grid, H, W, sr, sc):
    dist = [[-1]*W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque([(sr, sc)])
    dist[sr][sc] = 0
    while q:
        r, c = q.popleft()
        d = dist[r][c]
        for dr, dc in ((1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)):
            nr, nc = r+dr, c+dc
            if 0 <= nr < H and 0 <= nc < W and grid[nr][nc] != '#':
                if dist[nr][nc] == -1:
                    dist[nr][nc] = d + 1
                    q.append((nr, nc))
    return dist

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline

    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    sr = sc = gr = gc = -1
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            ch = grid[i][j]
            if ch == 'S':
                sr, sc = i, j
            elif ch == 'G':
                gr, gc = i, j
            elif ch == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    # Nodes: 0=start, 1..k=candies, k+1=goal
    k = len(candies)
    nodes = [(sr, sc)] + candies + [(gr, gc)]
    n = k + 2

    # Precompute shortest distances between all special nodes via BFS from each special node
    # Also compute dist from each node directly to goal.
    pair = [[INF]*n for _ in range(n)]
    for idx in range(n):
        r, c = nodes[idx]
        dist_grid = bfs_dist(grid, H, W, r, c)
        for jdx in range(n):
            rr, cc = nodes[jdx]
            dd = dist_grid[rr][cc]
            if dd != -1:
                pair[idx][jdx] = dd

    start_idx = 0
    goal_idx = n - 1

    # If even start->goal unreachable or >T, impossible
    if pair[start_idx][goal_idx] == INF or pair[start_idx][goal_idx] > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Bitmask DP:
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal cost to start from start, visit candies in mask, and end at node 'last'
    # where last is in 0..k-1 representing candy index (nodes = 1..k).
    # candies visited correspond exactly to bits set in mask.
    # Then feasibility for answer uses: dp + dist from last node to goal.
    # Also include possibility of visiting no candies (mask=0) ending at start.
    size = 1 << k
    # Use list-of-lists initialized to INF
    dp = [[INF]*k for _ in range(size)]

    # Initialize transitions to first candy
    for cidx in range(k):
        d = pair[start_idx][cidx+1]
        if d != INF and d <= T:  # still allow; final check handles goal leg too
            dp[1<<cidx][cidx] = d

    best = 0  # maximum candies
    # Feasibility for mask=0: directly start->goal
    if pair[start_idx][goal_idx] <= T:
        best = max(best, 0)

    # Held-Karp style DP
    for mask in range(size):
        # Quick pruning: if no state possible with this mask, skip
        # But computing this cheaply is complex; just let transitions check.
        for last in range(k):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # Try to extend to a new candy
            for nxt in range(k):
                if (mask >> nxt) & 1:
                    continue
                d = pair[last+1][nxt+1]
                if d == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | (1<<nxt)
                nd = cur + d
                # Don't compare with T here; final leg to goal matters, but cost so far should be bounded to avoid overflow
                if nd < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = nd

        # After building dp[mask][last], evaluate feasibility to finish at goal
        # maximize candies count among feasible states.
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= best:
            continue
        # Need check exists some last (including possibly start when mask=0 already handled).
        # For mask>0, consider end at each last in mask.
        for last in range(k):
            if ((mask >> last) & 1) == 0:
                continue
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            to_goal = pair[last+1][goal_idx]
            if to_goal == INF:
                continue
            if cur + to_goal <= T:
                best = cnt
                break

    # Special case: if k==0, dp arrays are empty; best already computed from start->goal.
    print(best)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()

```python
import sys
from collections import deque

def bfs_from(src, H, W, grid):
    INF = 10**18
    dist = [[INF] * W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque()
    sx, sy = src
    dist[sx][sy] = 0
    q.append((sx, sy))
    while q:
        x, y = q.popleft()
        d = dist[x][y]
        nd = d + 1
        for dx, dy in ((1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)):
            nx, ny = x + dx, y + dy
            if 0 <= nx < H and 0 <= ny < W and grid[nx][ny] != '#':
                if dist[nx][ny] > nd:
                    dist[nx][ny] = nd
                    q.append((nx, ny))
    return dist

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline
    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    s_pos = g_pos = None
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            if grid[i][j] == 'S':
                s_pos = (i, j)
            elif grid[i][j] == 'G':
                g_pos = (i, j)
            elif grid[i][j] == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    K = len(candies)  # <= 18
    # Nodes: 0 = S, 1..K = candies, K+1 = G
    nodes = [s_pos] + candies + [g_pos]
    N = K + 2

    # Precompute shortest distances between all special nodes
    # dist_special[a][b] = shortest moves from node a to node b, or INF if unreachable
    INF = 10**18
    dist_special = [[INF] * N for _ in range(N)]
    for a in range(N):
        dist_grid = bfs_from(nodes[a], H, W, grid)
        ax, ay = nodes[a]
        for b in range(N):
            bx, by = nodes[b]
            dist_special[a][b] = dist_grid[bx][by]

    start_to_goal = dist_special[0][N-1]
    if start_to_goal > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # DP over subsets of candies using Held-Karp style:
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal travel cost to start at S, visit candies in mask,
    # and end at candy "last" (last is index 0..K-1 referring to candies).
    # Transition uses pairwise distances between special nodes.
    # Answer is max popcount(mask) such that exists last with
    # dp[mask][last] + dist(last->G) <= T.
    size = 1 << K
    dp = [[INF] * K for _ in range(size)]

    # Initialize: visit a single candy
    for i in range(K):
        d = dist_special[0][i + 1]
        if d < INF:
            dp[1 << i][i] = d

    # Transitions
    for mask in range(size):
        for last in range(K):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # Try to add next candy
            for nxt in range(K):
                if mask >> nxt & 1:
                    continue
                d = dist_special[last + 1][nxt + 1]
                if d == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | (1 << nxt)
                val = cur + d
                if val < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = val

    # Also consider visiting no candy: just S->G
    best = 0
    if dist_special[0][N-1] <= T:
        best = 0

    # Check all states
    for mask in range(size):
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= best:
            continue
        for last in range(K):
            d = dp[mask][last]
            if d == INF:
                continue
            to_goal = dist_special[last + 1][N - 1]
            if to_goal == INF:
                continue
            if d + to_goal <= T:
                best = cnt
                break

    print(best)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()

<summary>Augmented generation 7</summary>

```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

INF = 10**18

def bfs_dist(grid, H, W, start):
    sr, sc = start
    dist = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque([(sr, sc)])
    dist[sr][sc] = 0
    while q:
        r, c = q.popleft()
        nd = dist[r][c] + 1
        if r > 0 and grid[r-1][c] != '#' and dist[r-1][c] == -1:
            dist[r-1][c] = nd
            q.append((r-1, c))
        if r + 1 < H and grid[r+1][c] != '#' and dist[r+1][c] == -1:
            dist[r+1][c] = nd
            q.append((r+1, c))
        if c > 0 and grid[r][c-1] != '#' and dist[r][c-1] == -1:
            dist[r][c-1] = nd
            q.append((r, c-1))
        if c + 1 < W and grid[r][c+1] != '#' and dist[r][c+1] == -1:
            dist[r][c+1] = nd
            q.append((r, c+1))
    return dist

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline

    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().rstrip()) for _ in range(H)]

    start = goal = None
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            if grid[i][j] == 'S':
                start = (i, j)
            elif grid[i][j] == 'G':
                goal = (i, j)
            elif grid[i][j] == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    n = len(candies)
    # Nodes: 0 = start, 1..n = candies, n+1 = goal
    nodes = [start] + candies + [goal]
    m = n + 2

    # Pairwise shortest distances between special nodes via BFS from each special node
    d = [[INF] * m for _ in range(m)]
    for a in range(m):
        distmap = bfs_dist(grid, H, W, nodes[a])
        ar, ac = nodes[a]
        for b in range(m):
            br, bc = nodes[b]
            dd = distmap[br][bc]
            if dd != -1:
                d[a][b] = dd

    # Quick impossibility: if start->goal unreachable within T, answer is -1
    if d[0][n+1] == INF or d[0][n+1] > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # DP: dp[mask][last] = minimal moves to start at 0, visit candies in mask, and end at candy last (0..n-1)
    # mask over n candies.
    # Initialize by going start -> each candy.
    size_mask = 1 << n
    dp = [[INF] * n for _ in range(size_mask)]

    for i in range(n):
        dist_si = d[0][i+1]
        if dist_si != INF and dist_si <= T:
            dp[1 << i][i] = dist_si

    # Transitions
    for mask in range(size_mask):
        # For each possible last in mask
        for last in range(n):
            if not (mask & (1 << last)):
                continue
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # try add next candy
            for nxt in range(n):
                if mask & (1 << nxt):
                    continue
                dist_last_nxt = d[last+1][nxt+1]
                if dist_last_nxt == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | (1 << nxt)
                nd = cur + dist_last_nxt
                if nd < dp[nmask][nxt] and nd <= T:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = nd

    # Evaluate answer:
    # Consider two cases:
    # 1) visit some candies and end at a candy last, then add distance last->goal
    # 2) visit zero candies: start->goal already checked
    ans = 0
    # zero candies already feasible => 0
    # But we want maximum candies, so compute over all dp states.
    for mask in range(size_mask):
        k = mask.bit_count()
        # If k <= ans skip? not necessarily because might tie; but we can if k <= ans then no need.
        if k <= ans:
            continue
        for last in range(n):
            if not (mask & (1 << last)):
                continue
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # must be able to go from last to goal within total T
            dist_last_goal = d[last+1][n+1]
            if dist_last_goal == INF:
                continue
            if cur + dist_last_goal <= T:
                ans = k
                break

    print(ans)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()

```python
import sys
from collections import deque

INF = 10**18

def bfs_from(start_r, start_c, H, W, grid):
    dist = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque([(start_r, start_c)])
    dist[start_r][start_c] = 0
    while q:
        r, c = q.popleft()
        d = dist[r][c]
        nd = d + 1
        if r > 0 and grid[r-1][c] != '#' and dist[r-1][c] == -1:
            dist[r-1][c] = nd
            q.append((r-1, c))
        if r+1 < H and grid[r+1][c] != '#' and dist[r+1][c] == -1:
            dist[r+1][c] = nd
            q.append((r+1, c))
        if c > 0 and grid[r][c-1] != '#' and dist[r][c-1] == -1:
            dist[r][c-1] = nd
            q.append((r, c-1))
        if c+1 < W and grid[r][c+1] != '#' and dist[r][c+1] == -1:
            dist[r][c+1] = nd
            q.append((r, c+1))
    return dist

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline

    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    sr = sc = gr = gc = -1
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            ch = grid[i][j]
            if ch == 'S':
                sr, sc = i, j
            elif ch == 'G':
                gr, gc = i, j
            elif ch == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    K = len(candies)  # <= 18
    # Nodes: 0 = S, 1..K = candies, K+1 = G
    nodes = [(sr, sc)] + candies + [(gr, gc)]
    M = K + 2

    # Pairwise distances between nodes via BFS from each node
    dist_mat = [[INF] * M for _ in range(M)]
    for idx in range(M):
        r0, c0 = nodes[idx]
        d = bfs_from(r0, c0, H, W, grid)
        for jdx in range(M):
            r1, c1 = nodes[jdx]
            dd = d[r1][c1]
            if dd != -1:
                dist_mat[idx][jdx] = dd

    # If can't reach goal from start in any <=T route, answer -1
    if dist_mat[0][K+1] > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Held-Karp style DP minimizing travel cost:
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal moves to start at S, visit candies in mask, and be at candy last
    # mask over K candies, last in [0..K-1] corresponds to candy index last.
    size = 1 << K
    dp = [[INF] * K for _ in range(size)]

    # Initialize: visit single candy i
    for i in range(K):
        d0 = dist_mat[0][i+1]
        if d0 != INF:
            dp[1 << i][i] = d0

    # Transitions
    # For efficiency, only iterate masks where dp non-INF transitions exist.
    for mask in range(size):
        # quick skip if mask has no reachable state
        # (still need check each last)
        for last in range(K):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # try go to next candy nxt
            rem = (~mask) & (size - 1)
            while rem:
                lsb = rem & -rem
                nxt = (lsb.bit_length() - 1)
                rem -= lsb
                d = dist_mat[last+1][nxt+1]
                if d == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | lsb
                cost = cur + d
                if cost < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = cost

    # Also allow visiting zero candies: finish cost is start->goal
    ans = 0
    # Evaluate each mask/last using true finish condition
    for mask in range(size):
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= ans:
            # still might be higher but skip if not
            pass
        for last in range(K):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            d_to_goal = dist_mat[last+1][K+1]
            if d_to_goal == INF:
                continue
            if cur + d_to_goal <= T:
                if cnt > ans:
                    ans = cnt

    # mask=0 (no candies) case:
    if dist_mat[0][K+1] <= T:
        ans = max(ans, 0)

    print(ans)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()
```

<summary>Augmented generation 9</summary>

```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

INF = 10**18

def bfs_from(start_idx, grid, H, W, sx, sy):
    dist = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
    q = deque()
    dist[sx][sy] = 0
    q.append((sx, sy))
    dirs = [(1,0),(-1,0),(0,1),(0,-1)]
    while q:
        x, y = q.popleft()
        d = dist[x][y]
        nd = d + 1
        for dx, dy in dirs:
            nx, ny = x + dx, y + dy
            if 0 <= nx < H and 0 <= ny < W and grid[nx][ny] != '#':
                if dist[nx][ny] == -1:
                    dist[nx][ny] = nd
                    q.append((nx, ny))
    return dist

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline
    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().strip()) for _ in range(H)]

    sx = sy = gx = gy = -1
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            c = grid[i][j]
            if c == 'S':
                sx, sy = i, j
            elif c == 'G':
                gx, gy = i, j
            elif c == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    N = len(candies)  # up to 18

    # special nodes: 0 = S, 1..N = candies, N+1 = G
    special = [(sx, sy)] + candies + [(gx, gy)]
    K = N + 2

    # compute pairwise shortest distances between special nodes
    # using BFS from each special node (grid up to 300x300)
    # Complexity: K * H*W, where K <= 20 => fine.
    pair = [[INF] * K for _ in range(K)]
    for a in range(K):
        x, y = special[a]
        dist_grid = bfs_from(a, grid, H, W, x, y)
        for b in range(K):
            tx, ty = special[b]
            d = dist_grid[tx][ty]
            if d != -1:
                pair[a][b] = d

    # If unreachable from S to G, answer is -1
    if pair[0][K-1] == INF or pair[0][K-1] > T:
        print(-1)
        return

    # Bitmask DP: visit candies subset, end at some candy (or directly at S)
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal cost to start at S, visit candies in mask, and end at candy last
    # last in 0..N-1 corresponds to that candy index.
    # We also allow mask=0 with "last = -1" concept by initializing dp for empty subset using S as base.
    size = 1 << N
    dp = [[INF] * N for _ in range(size)]

    # Initialize: visit one candy i
    for i in range(N):
        d = pair[0][1 + i]
        if d != INF and d <= T:  # cost so far doesn't need to be <=T but safe to prune a little
            dp[1 << i][i] = d

    # Transitions
    for mask in range(size):
        for last in range(N):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # add next candy nxt
            for nxt in range(N):
                bit = 1 << nxt
                if mask & bit:
                    continue
                nd = pair[1 + last][1 + nxt]
                if nd == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | bit
                cost = cur + nd
                if cost < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = cost

    # Evaluate best subset:
    # For subset mask ending at last, need cost(mask,last) + dist(last,G) <= T.
    # Also consider mask=0 (no candies): directly S->G already guaranteed feasible by earlier check.
    best = 0

    # no candies
    best = 0  # already feasible
    # subsets ending at some candy
    for mask in range(size):
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= best:
            # even if feasible, cannot beat best on candies count; but still might
            # allow early skipping only if strictly <= best
            continue
        for last in range(N):
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            to_goal = pair[1 + last][K - 1]
            if to_goal == INF:
                continue
            if cur + to_goal <= T:
                if cnt > best:
                    best = cnt
                    break  # for this mask, we already achieved max cnt

    print(best)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()
```

<summary>Augmented generation 10</summary>

```text
```python
import sys
from collections import deque

def solve():
    sys.setrecursionlimit(1_000_000)
    input = sys.stdin.readline

    H, W, T = map(int, input().split())
    grid = [list(input().rstrip()) for _ in range(H)]

    # Collect special nodes: start(0), candies(1..C), goal(last)
    sr = sc = gr = gc = -1
    candies = []
    for i in range(H):
        for j in range(W):
            if grid[i][j] == 'S':
                sr, sc = i, j
            elif grid[i][j] == 'G':
                gr, gc = i, j
            elif grid[i][j] == 'o':
                candies.append((i, j))

    C = len(candies)
    nodes = [(sr, sc)] + candies + [(gr, gc)]  # N = C + 2
    N = C + 2
    goal_idx = N - 1

    # BFS from each node to compute shortest distances on the grid
    # dist_u[v] gives distance between special nodes u->v, or INF if unreachable.
    INF = 10**18
    dist = [[INF] * N for _ in range(N)]

    # Precompute traversable cells check
    def bfs(si, sj, u):
        d = [[-1] * W for _ in range(H)]
        q = deque()
        q.append((si, sj))
        d[si][sj] = 0
        while q:
            r, c = q.popleft()
            nd = d[r][c] + 1
            if r > 0 and d[r-1][c] == -1 and grid[r-1][c] != '#':
                d[r-1][c] = nd
                q.append((r-1, c))
            if r + 1 < H and d[r+1][c] == -1 and grid[r+1][c] != '#':
                d[r+1][c] = nd
                q.append((r+1, c))
            if c > 0 and d[r][c-1] == -1 and grid[r][c-1] != '#':
                d[r][c-1] = nd
                q.append((r, c-1))
            if c + 1 < W and d[r][c+1] == -1 and grid[r][c+1] != '#':
                d[r][c+1] = nd
                q.append((r, c+1))
        for v, (ti, tj) in enumerate(nodes):
            if d[ti][tj] != -1:
                dist[u][v] = d[ti][tj]

    for u, (si, sj) in enumerate(nodes):
        bfs(si, sj, u)

    # If goal unreachable from start within T, still could be impossible: handle by DP feasibility.
    # DP over candies visited; Held–Karp style:
    # dp[mask][last] = minimal distance to start at S, visit candies in mask, end at candy last (index in candies list)
    # where last ranges 0..C-1. Use only minimal cost.
    if C == 0:
        ans = dist[0][goal_idx]
        if ans <= T:
            print(0)
        else:
            print(-1)
        return

    # Filter reachability: if some distances are INF, transitions will skip.
    # Precompute:
    d_start_to_cand = dist[0][1:1+C]             # size C
    d_cand_to_cand = [[INF]*C for _ in range(C)] # CxC
    for i in range(C):
        for j in range(C):
            d_cand_to_cand[i][j] = dist[1+i][1+j]
    d_cand_to_goal = [dist[1+i][goal_idx] for i in range(C)]

    M = 1 << C
    # dp arrays: list of dicts? But C<=18 => M<=262144, keep 2D with large INF? Use list-of-arrays.
    # We'll use dp = [ [INF]*C for _ in range(M) ] might be big: 262144*18 ~ 4.7M, ok.
    dp = [[INF] * C for _ in range(M)]

    # Initialize: masks with single candy i
    for i in range(C):
        if d_start_to_cand[i] != INF:
            dp[1 << i][i] = d_start_to_cand[i]

    best = -1
    # Iterate masks; for each, consider ending at each last.
    for mask in range(M):
        # quick pruning: maximum candies in mask
        cnt = mask.bit_count()
        if cnt <= best:
            # even if feasible, cannot beat best
            continue
        # find candidate end states
        # iterate last
        for last in range(C):
            if not (mask & (1 << last)):
                continue
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # Feasibility requires reaching goal after visiting this subset ending at last
            to_goal = d_cand_to_goal[last]
            if to_goal == INF:
                continue
            total = cur + to_goal
            if total <= T:
                if cnt > best:
                    best = cnt

        # Transitions: add a new candy next
        # Only if current mask could still exceed best (optional)
        if cnt + 1 <= best:
            continue
        for last in range(C):
            if not (mask & (1 << last)):
                continue
            cur = dp[mask][last]
            if cur == INF:
                continue
            # Try add next
            rem = ((M - 1) ^ mask)
            while rem:
                lsb = rem & -rem
                nxt = (lsb.bit_length() - 1)
                rem -= lsb
                nd = d_cand_to_cand[last][nxt]
                if nd == INF:
                    continue
                nmask = mask | (1 << nxt)
                new_cost = cur + nd
                if new_cost < dp[nmask][nxt]:
                    dp[nmask][nxt] = new_cost

    print(best if best != -1 else -1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    solve()
```

<summary>Score details for generation 5</summary>

```json
{
  "passed": 15,
  "total": 15,
  "cases": [
    {
      "passed": true,
      "expected": "1",
      "actual": "1",
